63 function resetSaveLabel() {

64 $("#confirmationMessage").removeClass("sucessfully-alert");

65 $("#confirmationMessage").removeClass("unsucessfully-alert");

66 $("#confirmationMessage").text("");

67 }

68 function saveSuccessful() {

69 resetSaveLabel();

70 $("#confirmationMessage").addClass("sucessfully-alert");

71 $("#confirmationMessage").text("Your request was sent. Thank you!");

72 $("#confirmationMessage").show();

73 $("#confirmationMessage").fadeIn("1000").delay(2000).fadeOut('1500').hide(0);

74 }

75 function saveUnsuccessful() {

76 resetSaveLabel();

77 $("#confirmationMessage").addClass("unsucessfully-alert");

78 $("#confirmationMessage").fadeIn("1000").delay(2000).fadeOut('1500').hide(0);

79 $("#confirmationMessage").text("Save operation not completed");

80 $("#confirmationMessage").show();

81 }

82 function setLotholdALot(e) {

83 logGAEvent("Hold-a-Lot", "ISP", "popup-open_HL");

84 holdALotInternalReference = e.dataset.internalreference;

85 }

87 function setGAEvent() {

88 requestInfoSource = "Lot";

89 logGAEvent("Request-Info-lot", "ISP", "Request-info-popup-open_l");

90 }

95 }

97 document.getElementById('isp-external-link-iframe').setAttribute('src', e.dataset.link);

99 }

290 var ajaxCallStatus = {

291 Accepted: 1,

292 Error: 2

293 }

294 $('#requestForm').on('submit', function (e) {

295 e.preventDefault();

296 if ($('#requestForm').valid()) {

297 var formValues = $('form').serializeArray();

298 $('.btn.btn-primary').button('loading');

299 $('.validation-summary-errors').find('li').css('display', 'none');

300 $('.validation-summary-errors').addClass('validation-summary-valid').removeClass('validation-summary-errors');

301 var siteId = getParameterByName('siteID');

302 let lotids = sessionStorage.getItem(siteId);

303 if (lotids != null && lotids.trim() != "") {

304 for (var i = 0; i < formValues.length; i++) {

305 if (formValues[i].name == "Comments") {

306 formValues[i].value = formValues[i].value + "\nLotids: " + lotids;

307 }

308 }

309 }

310 var platformType = {};

311 platformType.name = 'Platform';

312 platformType.value = JSON.stringify(5);

313 formValues.push(platformType);

314 $.ajax({

315 url: '/Prospects/AddProspect',

316 type: 'post',

317 data: formValues,

318 success: function (data) {

319 if (typeof (data) != "undefined" && typeof (data.ajaxCallStatus) != "undefined" && data.ajaxCallStatus == ajaxCallStatus.Error) {

320 if ($('.zipCodeError').length == 0 && $('.validation-summary-valid ul').length > 0) {

321 $('.validation-summary-valid ul').append('<li class="zipCodeError">The Zip Code field is required.</li>');

322 $('.validation-summary-valid').addClass('validation-summary-errors').removeClass('validation-summary-valid');

323 }

324 else {

325 $('.validation-summary-valid ul').append('<li class="zipCodeError">The Zip Code field is required.</li>');

326 }

327 } else {

328 $('#myModal').modal('toggle');

329 document.getElementById('requestForm').reset();

330 showSuccessModel();

331 switch (requestInfoSource) {

332 case "Right": logGAEvent("Request-Info-right", "ISP", "form-submit_r");

333 break;

334 case "Bottom": logGAEvent("Request-Info-bottom", "ISP", "form-submit");

335 break;

336 case "Lot": logGAEvent("Request-Info-lot", "ISP", "form-submit_l");

337 break;

338 }

339 }

340 $('.btn.btn-primary').button('reset');

341 },

342 error: function (data) {

343 saveUnsuccessful();

344 $('.btn.btn-primary').button('reset');

345 }

346 })

347 }

348 });

349 $('#myModal').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {

350 $('.validation-summary-errors').addClass('validation-summary-valid').removeClass('validation-summary-errors').find('li').remove();

351 document.getElementById('requestForm').reset();

352 $('.btn.btn-primary').button('reset');

353 });

354

355 $(".close-ri-modal").on('click', function () {

356 switch (requestInfoSource) {

357 case "Right": logGAEvent("Request-Info-right", "ISP", " Request-info-popup-close_r");

358 break;

359 case "Bottom": logGAEvent("Request-Info-bottom", "ISP", "Request-info-popup-close");

360 break;

361 case "Lot": logGAEvent("Request-Info-lot", "ISP", "Request-info-popup-close_l");

362 break;

363 }

364 });
